2235 <p>The Blanco Precis 32" Granite Single-Basin Kitchen sink is a large undermount sink made of white granite composite. Silgranit, a material that is 80% granite, is extra-durable and designed to prevent scratches, stains, and heat damage up to 536 degrees. The straightforward design includes a 9.5" basin depth, deep enough and wide enough to hold a wide array of dishes and pots and pans of various sizes.</p>

2238 </p>

2239 <p>The Precis collection from Blanco features sinks made of Silgranite, an 80% granite composite material designed to withstand scratches, stains, and heat up to 536 degrees. Sinks in the Precis collection are available in a wide range of colors, shapes, and sizes.</p>

Blanco sinks include undermount, dual-mount, and drop-in install styles in addition to single and double-basin designs.</p>
